## Executive Summary

**PureTask** is a **two-sided marketplace platform** that connects **clients** (homeowners, businesses, Airbnb hosts) with **professional cleaners** through a sophisticated, trust-based booking system. Built on React + Base44 BaaS (Backend-as-a-Service), it features advanced reliability scoring, GPS tracking, photo verification, credit-based payments, and AI-powered automation.

### Key Differentiators:
- âœ… **Reliability Scoring System** - Performance-based tier pricing (0-100 scale)
- âœ… **GPS + Photo Verification** - 100% accountability on every job
- âœ… **Pay-After-Approval** - Client-first trust model (18hr auto-approve)
- âœ… **AI-Powered Matching** - Smart cleaner suggestions (20% reliability weight)
- âœ… **Credit-Based Economy** - Psychological pricing advantage (10 credits = $1)
- âœ… **Pet-Friendly Platform** - Automatic $30 pet fee system

### Current Status:
- **Production-Ready Codebase** - 118 pages, 500+ components
- **Professional Error Handling** - 171 files updated
- **Smart Caching System** - 60% fewer API calls
- **Rate Limiting Protection** - Abuse prevention active
- **100% Test Coverage** - 57 tests passing on core utilities

### Revenue Model (Updated):
- **15-20% platform fee** from completed bookings
- **10% instant cash-out fee** (increased revenue stream)
- **$30 pet fee** per booking (new revenue)
- **Memberships & bundles** (recurring revenue)
- **Cleaners earn 80-85%** of booking price

---

## ğŸ¯ What is PureTask?

### Core Business Model

PureTask is a **"Trust-First" cleaning marketplace** solving the fundamental problem in gig economy cleaning: **How do you ensure quality and accountability without direct supervision?**

### The Complete Solution

#### 1. **Verified Cleaners**
- **Background checks** via Checkr ($35/cleaner, reimbursed after 10 jobs)
- **KYC verification** (government ID + selfie match)
- **Identity verification** (phone, email, address)
- **Bank account verification** (micro-deposit confirmation)

#### 2. **Reliability Scoring** (0-100 scale)
- Dynamic performance tracking
- Real-time updates after each job
- Automatic tier assignment
- Transparent scoring breakdown

#### 3. **GPS Check-In/Out**
- Proof of attendance (within 100m radius)
- Punctuality tracking (within 15 minutes)
- GPS coordinates stored for disputes
- Real-time client notifications

#### 4. **Photo Verification**
- Before/after photos required (minimum 2 each)
- Timestamp + GPS embedded in metadata
- Side-by-side comparison view
- Quality assurance evidence

#### 5. **Pay-After-Approval** (18hr window)
- Client approves work before payment releases
- **Auto-approval after 18 hours** (updated from 48hr)
- Credits held (not charged) until approval
- Dispute window during review period

#### 6. **Tier-Based Pricing**
- Performance determines rates ($15-85/hr)
- 4 tiers: Developing, Semi Pro, Pro, Elite
- Automatic tier promotions/demotions
- Clear progression path for cleaners

#### 7. **Pet-Friendly System** (NEW)
- Simple yes/no question during booking
- **Automatic $30 fee** if client has pets
- Applied to all bookings with pets
- Transparent pricing (shown before payment)

### Market Opportunity

**Target Market:**
- **$46B U.S. cleaning services market** (2026)
- **78 million households** with dual-income families
- **5.6 million Airbnb listings** (40% have pets!)
- **Growing gig economy** (cleaners seeking flexibility)

**Problem We Solve:**

**For Clients:**
- âŒ Trust issues with strangers in home
- âŒ Quality inconsistency (no verification)
- âŒ No accountability (cleaners ghost)
- âŒ Opaque pricing (hidden fees)
- âœ… **PureTask Solution:** GPS + photos + reliability scoring + transparent pricing

**For Cleaners:**
- âŒ Low pay (exploitative companies)
- âŒ No recognition for quality work
- âŒ No career progression path
- âŒ Late payments (or no payment at all)
- âœ… **PureTask Solution:** Performance-based tiers + 80-85% earnings + weekly payouts

**For Pet Owners (40% of market):**
- âŒ Hard to find pet-friendly cleaners
- âŒ Last-minute upcharges
- âŒ Cleaners who are afraid of pets
- âœ… **PureTask Solution:** Pet-friendly badge + transparent $30 fee + pet specialty tags

- **Airbnb Hosts** - Fast turnaround cleaning (3-4 hour window)
- **Retirees** - Want trusted, consistent help, same cleaner preferred
- **Small Businesses** - Office cleaning needs, after-hours service

**STEP 3: Backend Processing**
```javascript
// Automatic fee calculation (backend)
function calculateBookingPrice(bookingData) {
  let total = 0;
  
  // Base rate calculation
  total += bookingData.hourly_rate * bookingData.hours;
  
  // Add-on calculation (deep/moveout)
  if (bookingData.cleaning_type === 'deep') {
    total += bookingData.deep_addon_rate * bookingData.hours;
  } else if (bookingData.cleaning_type === 'moveout') {
    total += bookingData.moveout_addon_rate * bookingData.hours;
  }
  
  // PET FEE (NEW - AUTOMATIC)
  if (bookingData.has_pets === true) {
    total += 300; // $30 = 300 credits
    bookingData.pet_fee = 300;
  } else {
    bookingData.pet_fee = 0;
  }
  
  // Additional services
  total += calculateAdditionalServices(bookingData.additional_services);
  
  return {
    subtotal: total,
    pet_fee: bookingData.pet_fee,
    breakdown: {
      base: bookingData.hourly_rate * bookingData.hours,
      addon: getAddonCost(bookingData),
      pet_fee: bookingData.pet_fee,
      additional: calculateAdditionalServices()
    }
  };
}
```

##### **4. Smart Matching Algorithm** (UPDATED WEIGHTS)

**AI-Powered Suggestions based on:**

```
MATCHING FORMULA (Updated V3.0):
â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•

Match Score = 
  (Distance Ã— 20%) +            [REDUCED from 25%]
  (Availability Ã— 20%) +        [MAINTAINED]
  (Reliability Ã— 20%) +         [INCREASED from 15%] â­
  (Pricing Ã— 10%) +             [MAINTAINED]
  (Rating Ã— 10%) +              [MAINTAINED]
  (Tier Ã— 7%) +                 [INCREASED from 5%]

**Detailed Factor Explanations:**

**1. DISTANCE (20% weight)**
```
HOW IT'S CALCULATED:
â”œâ”€ Google Maps API: Driving distance
â”œâ”€ Optimal range: 0-15 miles
â”œâ”€ Score drops linearly after 15 miles
â””â”€ Max distance: 25 miles (hard limit)

SCORING:
â”œâ”€ 0-5 miles: 100% score (1.0)
â”œâ”€ 5-10 miles: 80% score (0.8)
â”œâ”€ 10-15 miles: 60% score (0.6)
â”œâ”€ 15-20 miles: 40% score (0.4)
â”œâ”€ 20-25 miles: 20% score (0.2)
â””â”€ >25 miles: 0% (not shown)

WHY IT MATTERS:
â”œâ”€ Shorter distance = Cleaner more likely to accept
â”œâ”€ Lower travel costs for cleaner
â”œâ”€ Less cancellations due to traffic
â””â”€ Better environmental impact
```

**2. AVAILABILITY (20% weight)**
```
HOW IT'S CALCULATED:
â”œâ”€ Cleaner's calendar checked for exact date/time
â”œâ”€ Buffer time added (30min before/after)
â”œâ”€ Max daily bookings checked
â””â”€ Blackout dates excluded

SCORING:
â”œâ”€ Available exactly: 100% score (1.0)
â”œâ”€ Available Â±1 hour: 80% score (0.8)
â”œâ”€ Available same day: 60% score (0.6)
â”œâ”€ Available same week: 40% score (0.4)
â””â”€ Not available: 0% (not shown)

WHY IT MATTERS:
â”œâ”€ Guaranteed cleaner can accept
â”œâ”€ No back-and-forth scheduling
â”œâ”€ Instant booking confirmation
â””â”€ Higher client satisfaction
```

**3. RELIABILITY SCORE (20% weight) - INCREASED â­**
```
HOW IT'S CALCULATED:
â”œâ”€ Cleaner's current reliability score (0-100)
â”œâ”€ Normalized to 0-1 scale
â”œâ”€ Score / 100 = Factor
â””â”€ Factor Ã— 20% = Contribution

SCORING EXAMPLES:
â”œâ”€ 95 score (Elite): 95/100 Ã— 20% = 19% contribution
â”œâ”€ 80 score (Pro): 80/100 Ã— 20% = 16% contribution
â”œâ”€ 65 score (Semi Pro): 65/100 Ã— 20% = 13% contribution
â”œâ”€ 45 score (Developing): 45/100 Ã— 20% = 9% contribution
â””â”€ New cleaner (50): 50/100 Ã— 20% = 10% contribution

WHY INCREASED TO 20%:
â”œâ”€ Reliability is CORE to trust model
â”œâ”€ Higher weight = Elite cleaners ranked higher
â”œâ”€ Encourages cleaners to maintain performance
â”œâ”€ Clients get better matches
â””â”€ Reduces disputes and refunds

IMPACT ON RANKINGS:
Before (15% weight):
1. John (Distance: 5mi, Score: 70) = 78% match
2. Sarah (Distance: 10mi, Score: 90) = 76% match

After (20% weight):
1. Sarah (Distance: 10mi, Score: 90) = 80% match â¬†
2. John (Distance: 5mi, Score: 70) = 76% match â¬‡

Result: Higher-performing cleaner now ranks #1!
```

##### **5. Multi-Booking System**

**How It Works:**
```
CLIENT WANTS: Weekly cleaning for 4 weeks

OPTION 1: Book Individually
â”œâ”€ 4 separate bookings
â”œâ”€ 4 separate payments
â”œâ”€ No discount
â””â”€ Total: 1,600 credits ($160)

OPTION 2: Multi-Booking (RECOMMENDED)
â”œâ”€ 1 booking request with 4 dates
â”œâ”€ Same cleaner all 4 times
â”œâ”€ 10% bulk discount applied
â”œâ”€ 1 upfront payment
â””â”€ Total: 1,440 credits ($144) - SAVE $16!

BOOKING PROCESS:
1. Select "Multi-Booking" option
2. Choose 4+ dates on calendar
3. System checks cleaner availability for ALL dates
4. Only shows cleaners available all 4 times
5. Automatic discount applied
6. Single payment (all 4 bookings)
7. Credits released per job after approval
```

**Benefits:**
- âœ… **Client:** 10% discount, guaranteed cleaner, convenient
- âœ… **Cleaner:** Guaranteed income, relationship building
- âœ… **Platform:** Higher LTV, lower acquisition cost

##### **6. Recurring Bookings**

**How It Works:**
```
CLIENT WANTS: Same cleaner every Tuesday at 10am

SETUP PROCESS:
1. Complete first booking
2. After approval, prompt appears:
   "Love [Cleaner Name]? Book them weekly and save 10%!"
3. Select frequency:
   â”œâ”€ Weekly (every 7 days)
   â”œâ”€ Biweekly (every 14 days)
   â””â”€ Monthly (every 30 days)
4. Set start date and end date (or "Until I cancel")
5. Auto-debit enabled (credits auto-deducted)
6. Bookings auto-generated

AUTO-GENERATION:
â”œâ”€ System creates booking 7 days in advance
â”œâ”€ Cleaner auto-accepts (if enabled in settings)
â”œâ”€ Client notified 48hrs before
â”œâ”€ Credits auto-held 24hrs before
â””â”€ Normal approval process after completion

MANAGEMENT:
â”œâ”€ Pause anytime (up to 3 months)
â”œâ”€ Skip specific dates (vacations)
â”œâ”€ Change frequency
â”œâ”€ Change time/day
â””â”€ Cancel (2-week notice required)
```

```

## ğŸ’³ FINANCIAL SYSTEMS - EXPLAINED IN DETAIL

### A. CREDIT SYSTEM (Complete Breakdown)

#### **Core Principle:**
**10 credits = $1 USD** (or 1 credit = $0.10)

**Why Credits Instead of Dollars?**

```
PSYCHOLOGICAL BENEFITS:
â”œâ”€ Less painful to spend "credits" than "dollars"
â”œâ”€ Gamification (earn bonuses, levels, rewards)
â”œâ”€ Easy fractional amounts (375 credits vs $37.50)
â””â”€ Platform lock-in (sunk cost fallacy)

OPERATIONAL BENEFITS:
â”œâ”€ Easy to grant promotional credits
â”œâ”€ Precise pricing (no decimal confusion)
â”œâ”€ Universal currency across features
â””â”€ Prevents chargebacks (non-refundable to card)

FINANCIAL BENEFITS:
â”œâ”€ Float on purchased credits (time value of money)
â”œâ”€ Breakage (unused credits = profit)
â”œâ”€ Upsell opportunities (buy more, get bonus)
â””â”€ Recurring revenue (auto-refill)
```

#### **Credit Sources - DETAILED EXPLANATION**

**1. PURCHASES (Primary Source)**
```
HOW IT WORKS:
Step 1: Client clicks "Buy Credits"
Step 2: Selects package
Step 3: Stripe processes credit card
Step 4: Webhook confirms payment
Step 5: Credits added to wallet instantly

PACKAGES:
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚  ğŸ’³ CREDIT PACKAGES                     â”‚
â”œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¤
â”‚  500 credits   = $50    (0% bonus)      â”‚
â”‚  1,000 credits = $95    (5% bonus)      â”‚
â”‚  2,500 credits = $225   (10% bonus)     â”‚
â”‚  5,000 credits = $425   (15% bonus)     â”‚
â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜

BONUS CALCULATION:
500 credits:
â”œâ”€ Pay: $50
â”œâ”€ Get: 500 credits
â”œâ”€ Bonus: 0 credits (0%)
â””â”€ Effective rate: $0.10/credit

1,000 credits:
â”œâ”€ Pay: $95
â”œâ”€ Get: 1,000 credits
â”œâ”€ Bonus: 50 credits (5%)
â””â”€ Effective rate: $0.095/credit (5% off)

â”œâ”€ Pay: $225
â”œâ”€ Get: 2,500 credits
â”œâ”€ Bonus: 250 credits (10%)
â””â”€ Effective rate: $0.09/credit (10% off)

5,000 credits:
â”œâ”€ Pay: $425
â”œâ”€ Get: 5,000 credits
â”œâ”€ Bonus: 750 credits (15%)
â””â”€ Effective rate: $0.085/credit (15% off)

WHY BONUSES WORK:
â”œâ”€ Incentivizes larger purchases
â”œâ”€ Higher customer lifetime value
â”œâ”€ Better retention (more credits = more bookings)
â””â”€ Lower transaction costs (1 big vs many small)

REVENUE IMPLICATIONS:
â”œâ”€ Bonuses reduce margin slightly
â”œâ”€ BUT: Higher average purchase size
â”œâ”€ AND: Lower Stripe fees (% savings on volume)
â””â”€ NET: More profitable per client
```

```

PROCESS:

   â”œâ”€ Before/after photos

   â”œâ”€ Message history
   â”œâ”€ Cleaner's reliability score
   â””â”€ Past performance of both parties

6. Credits refunded to wallet
7. Both parties notified

EXAMPLE:

## ğŸ” VERIFICATION & SECURITY SYSTEMS - DETAILED

### A. BACKGROUND CHECK SYSTEM (Complete Explanation)

#### **What is a Background Check?**

A background check is a comprehensive screening process that verifies a person's identity and checks for any criminal history, ensuring they are safe to work in clients' homes.

#### **Background Check Process - Step by Step**

```

**Why This System Works:**

```
âœ… BENEFITS FOR CLEANERS:
â”œâ”€ Low barrier to entry ($35 vs $100+ elsewhere)
â”œâ”€ Reimbursed if committed (not a sunk cost)
â”œâ”€ Clear goal (10 jobs = get money back)
â””â”€ Fair incentive (rewards dedication)

âœ… BENEFITS FOR PURETASK:
â”œâ”€ Filters serious cleaners (commitment test)
â”œâ”€ Covers background check costs
â”œâ”€ Revenue from dropouts (30% don't complete)
â”œâ”€ Quality control (only committed cleaners stay)
â””â”€ Competitive advantage (others don't reimburse)

âœ… BENEFITS FOR CLIENTS:
â”œâ”€ Only serious cleaners on platform
â”œâ”€ All cleaners background-checked
â”œâ”€ Higher quality service (committed pros)
â””â”€ Safer homes (verified cleaners)
```

### B. MICRO-DEPOSIT VERIFICATION (Banking)

#### **What is Micro-Deposit Verification?**

Micro-deposit verification is a bank account authentication method where two small deposits (usually $0.01-$0.99) are sent to a bank account, and the account holder must verify the exact amounts to prove ownership.

#### **How Micro-Deposit Verification Works**

```
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚  ğŸ¦ MICRO-DEPOSIT VERIFICATION PROCESS  â”‚
â”œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¤
â”‚  STEP 1: CLEANER PROVIDES BANK INFO     â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Routing number (9 digits)           â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Account number                      â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Account type (checking/savings)     â”‚
â”‚  â””â”€ Account holder name                 â”‚
â”‚                                         â”‚
â”‚  STEP 2: STRIPE SENDS MICRO-DEPOSITS    â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Stripe (via Plaid) initiates        â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Two deposits sent:                  â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”œâ”€ Deposit #1: $0.32 (example)      â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â””â”€ Deposit #2: $0.45 (example)      â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Amounts are random (< $1 each)      â”‚
â”‚  â””â”€ Takes 1-2 business days to appear   â”‚
â”‚                                         â”‚
â”‚  STEP 3: CLEANER CHECKS BANK STATEMENT  â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Logs into bank account              â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Views recent transactions           â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Sees two deposits from "STRIPE"     â”‚
â”‚  â””â”€ Notes the exact amounts             â”‚
â”‚                                         â”‚
â”‚  STEP 4: CLEANER VERIFIES AMOUNTS       â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Returns to PureTask                 â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Enters two deposit amounts:         â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”œâ”€ Amount 1: $0.32                  â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â””â”€ Amount 2: $0.45                  â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Clicks "Verify"                     â”‚
â”‚  â””â”€ System validates amounts            â”‚
â”‚                                         â”‚
â”‚  STEP 5: VERIFICATION COMPLETE          â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ If correct: "Bank verified! âœ…"     â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ If incorrect: "Try again (2 more    â”‚
â”‚      attempts)"                         â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Verified badge on profile           â”‚
â”‚  â””â”€ Can now receive payouts             â”‚
â”‚                                         â”‚
â”‚  STEP 6: MICRO-DEPOSITS REVERSED        â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Stripe withdraws the two deposits   â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ -$0.32 and -$0.45 appear            â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Net effect: $0 (no cost!)           â”‚
â”‚  â””â”€ Verification complete               â”‚
â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜
```

#### **Visual Example**

```
CLEANER'S BANK STATEMENT:

DATE     | DESCRIPTION            | AMOUNT
---------|------------------------|----------
01/01/26 | Starting Balance       | $1,250.00
01/02/26 | STRIPE VERIFICATION    | +$0.32
01/02/26 | STRIPE VERIFICATION    | +$0.45
01/03/26 | Grocery Store          | -$45.23

### A. MEMBERSHIP TIERS (Complete Breakdown)

#### **What Are Membership Tiers?**

Membership tiers are subscription-based premium features that provide clients with enhanced benefits, discounts, and priority service in exchange for a monthly fee.

â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜
```

### **How Membership is Assessed & Enforced**

#### **Assessment (How It's Tracked)**

```
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚  ğŸ“Š MEMBERSHIP TRACKING SYSTEM          â”‚
â”œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¤
â”‚  DATABASE FIELDS:                       â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ membership_tier: "basic" | "premium"â”‚
â”‚  â”‚   | "vip"                            â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ membership_status: "active" |       â”‚
â”‚  â”‚   "cancelled" | "expired"            â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ membership_start_date: "2026-01-01" â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ membership_expiry: "2026-02-01"     â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ stripe_subscription_id: "sub_xyz"   â”‚
â”‚  â””â”€ auto_renew: true | false            â”‚
â”‚                                         â”‚
â”‚  REAL-TIME CHECKS:                      â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Every booking: Check tier status    â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Apply discount if premium/VIP       â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Multiply loyalty points             â”‚
â”‚  â””â”€ Enforce cancellation policy         â”‚
â”‚                                         â”‚
â”‚  DAILY CRON JOB:                        â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Check expiring memberships          â”‚

â”‚  â””â”€ Downgrade expired accounts          â”‚
â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜
```

#### **Enforcement (How Benefits Are Applied)**

**1. BOOKING DISCOUNT ENFORCEMENT**
```javascript
// Backend code - Automatic discount application
function calculateBookingPrice(bookingData, clientProfile) {
  let subtotal = calculateBasePrice(bookingData);
  
  // Check membership tier
  if (clientProfile.membership_tier === 'premium' && 
      clientProfile.membership_status === 'active') {
    // Apply 5% discount
    const discount = subtotal * 0.05;
    subtotal -= discount;
    bookingData.discount_applied = discount;
    bookingData.discount_reason = "Premium Member 5% Off";
  } 
  else if (clientProfile.membership_tier === 'vip' && 
           clientProfile.membership_status === 'active') {
    // Apply 10% discount
    const discount = subtotal * 0.10;
    subtotal -= discount;
    bookingData.discount_applied = discount;
    bookingData.discount_reason = "VIP Member 10% Off";
    
    // Waive booking fee for VIP
    bookingData.booking_fee = 0;
    bookingData.fee_waived = true;
  }
  
  return subtotal;
}
```

**2. LOYALTY POINTS MULTIPLIER**
```javascript
// After booking approval - Award points
function awardLoyaltyPoints(booking, clientProfile) {
  const basePoints = booking.final_price; // 1 point per credit
  
  // Apply multiplier based on tier
  let multiplier = 1;
  if (clientProfile.membership_tier === 'premium') {
    multiplier = 2;
  } else if (clientProfile.membership_tier === 'vip') {
    multiplier = 3;
  }
  
  const totalPoints = basePoints * multiplier;
  
  // Add to client's loyalty balance
  clientProfile.loyalty_points += totalPoints;
  
  // Log transaction
  LoyaltyTransaction.create({
    client_email: clientProfile.user_email,
    points: totalPoints,
    multiplier: multiplier,
    reason: `Booking #${booking.id} (${multiplier}x ${clientProfile.membership_tier})`,
    created_at: new Date()
  });
}
```

**3. CANCELLATION POLICY ENFORCEMENT**
```javascript
// When client requests cancellation
function processCancellation(booking, clientProfile) {
  const now = new Date();
  const bookingDate = new Date(booking.date + ' ' + booking.start_time);
  const hoursUntilBooking = (bookingDate - now) / (1000 * 60 * 60);
  
  // Determine refund based on membership tier
  let refundPercent = 0;
  let policyHours = 48; // Default: Basic tier
  
  if (clientProfile.membership_tier === 'premium') {
    policyHours = 24;
  } else if (clientProfile.membership_tier === 'vip') {
    policyHours = 12;
  }
  
  if (hoursUntilBooking >= policyHours) {
    // Full refund within policy window
    refundPercent = 100;
  } else {
    // No refund (within cancellation window)
    refundPercent = 0;
  }
  
  return {
    refund_percent: refundPercent,
    refund_amount: booking.total_price * (refundPercent / 100),
    reason: `Cancelled ${hoursUntilBooking.toFixed(1)}hrs before (${policyHours}hr policy for ${clientProfile.membership_tier})`
  };
}
```

**4. PRIORITY SUPPORT ENFORCEMENT**
```javascript
// Support ticket creation
function createSupportTicket(clientProfile, issue) {
  const ticket = {
    client_email: clientProfile.user_email,
    issue: issue,
    created_at: new Date(),
    status: 'open'
  };
  
  // Set priority based on membership
  if (clientProfile.membership_tier === 'vip') {
    ticket.priority = 'urgent'; // 1-hour SLA
    ticket.assigned_to = clientProfile.dedicated_manager; // Named person
    ticket.communication_channel = ['email', 'phone', 'text'];
  } else if (clientProfile.membership_tier === 'premium') {
    ticket.priority = 'high'; // 4-hour SLA
    ticket.assigned_to = 'premium_queue';
    ticket.communication_channel = ['email', 'sms'];
  } else {
    ticket.priority = 'normal'; // 24-hour SLA
    ticket.assigned_to = 'general_queue';
    ticket.communication_channel = ['email'];
  }
  
  // Send to appropriate queue
  SupportTicket.create(ticket);
  
  // Notify support team
  notifySupportTeam(ticket);
}
```

**5. SAME-DAY BOOKING PRIORITY**
```javascript
// Smart matching algorithm - Priority boost
function calculateMatchScore(cleaner, booking, clientProfile) {
  let baseScore = calculateBaseMatchScore(cleaner, booking);
  
  // Same-day booking adjustment
  const isSameDay = isSameDayBooking(booking.date);
  
  if (isSameDay) {
    if (clientProfile.membership_tier === 'vip') {
      // VIP: Guaranteed same-day (top of list)
      baseScore += 50; // Massive boost ensures #1 ranking
    } else if (clientProfile.membership_tier === 'premium') {
      // Premium: Priority (higher ranking)
      baseScore += 20; // Significant boost
    }
    // Basic: No boost (standard ranking)
  }
  
  return baseScore;
}
```

### B. LOYALTY PROGRAM (Complete Explanation)

#### **What is the Loyalty Program?**

The loyalty program rewards clients with points for every booking and other actions, which can be redeemed for credits (money) to use on future bookings.

#### **How Points Are Earned**

```
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”

â”‚  1. BOOKING SPENDING (Primary)          â”‚

#### **How Points Are Redeemed**

```
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”

â”‚                                         â”‚

â”‚  â€¢ No maximum                           â”‚
â”‚                                         â”‚

â”‚  5. Credits added to wallet instantly   â”‚
â”‚  6. Points deducted from balance        â”‚
â”‚                                         â”‚
â”‚  RESTRICTIONS:                          â”‚
â”‚  â€¢ Points never expire                  â”‚
â”‚  â€¢ Redeemed credits expire in 2 years   â”‚
â”‚  â€¢ Cannot transfer points to others     â”‚
â”‚  â€¢ Cannot redeem points for cash        â”‚
â”‚  â€¢ Must be used on PureTask platform    â”‚
â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜
```

### C. REFERRAL PROGRAM (Explained in Detail)

#### **What is the Referral Program?**

The referral program incentivizes existing clients to invite friends to PureTask by offering both parties 250 credits ($25) when the friend completes their first booking.

#### **How It Works (Step-by-Step)**

```
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”

#### **"Client Refers Client" - Clarification**

**Question:** You mentioned "Client refers client: Both get 250 credits" AND "Referral Program: Client refers client: Both get 250 credits" - are these the same thing?

**Answer:** YES! They are the same program. Here's the clarification:

```
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚  ğŸ“ TERMINOLOGY CLARIFICATION            â”‚
â”œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¤

â”‚                                         â”‚

â”‚    booking                              â”‚
â”‚                                         â”‚

â”‚  â€¢ Marketing clarity (different contextsâ”‚
â”‚  â€¢ "Referral Program" = Official name   â”‚

## âš–ï¸ DISPUTE RESOLUTION SYSTEM - EXPLAINED IN DETAIL

### **What is a Dispute?**

A dispute is a formal complaint filed by a client when they believe the cleaning service was unsatisfactory, incomplete, or the cleaner failed to show up. It triggers an investigation process that can result in a full refund, partial refund, or denial of refund.

### **Complete Dispute Workflow**

```
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚  âš–ï¸ DISPUTE RESOLUTION WORKFLOW (STEP-BY-STEP)                  â”‚
â”œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¤
â”‚  STEP 1: CLIENT OPENS DISPUTE (Within 18hr Window)              â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Client clicks "Open Dispute" on booking                     â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Selects dispute reason:                                     â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”œâ”€ âŒ No-Show (cleaner never arrived)                       â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”œâ”€ âš ï¸ Quality Issues (cleaning not thorough)                â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”œâ”€ â° Late Arrival (>30 minutes late)                       â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”œâ”€ ğŸš« Incomplete Work (didn't finish agreed tasks)          â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”œâ”€ ğŸ’” Damage (broke/damaged something)                      â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â””â”€ ğŸ“ Other (free text description)                         â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Uploads evidence:                                           â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”œâ”€ Photos (up to 10)                                        â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”œâ”€ Videos (optional)                                        â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â””â”€ Written description (500 chars max)                      â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Selects desired resolution:                                 â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”œâ”€ Full refund (100% credits back)                          â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”œâ”€ Partial refund (suggest amount)                          â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”œâ”€ Free rebook (different cleaner)                          â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â””â”€ Other (explain)                                          â”‚
â”‚  â””â”€ Submits dispute                                             â”‚
â”‚                                                                 â”‚
â”‚  SYSTEM ACTIONS:                                                â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Auto-approval PAUSED (18hr timer stopped)                   â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Credits remain held (not charged)                           â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Cleaner payout frozen                                       â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Admin team notified                                         â”‚
â”‚  â””â”€ Dispute ID assigned (DSP-2026-001)                          â”‚
â”‚                                                                 â”‚
â”‚  STEP 2: CLEANER NOTIFIED (24hr Response Window)                â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Email sent: "Dispute opened for Booking #ABC123"            â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ SMS alert: "Urgent: Client opened dispute"                  â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Push notification: "Respond within 24 hours"                â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ In-app notification: Red badge on dashboard                 â”‚
â”‚  â””â”€ Shows dispute details:                                      â”‚
â”‚     â”œâ”€ Client's reason                                          â”‚
â”‚     â”œâ”€ Client's evidence (photos)                               â”‚
â”‚     â”œâ”€ Requested resolution                                     â”‚
â”‚     â””â”€ Response deadline                                        â”‚
â”‚                                                                 â”‚
â”‚  STEP 3: CLEANER RESPONDS (Within 24hrs)                        â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Clicks "Respond to Dispute"                                 â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Writes response (explaining their side)                     â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Uploads counter-evidence:                                   â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”œâ”€ Before/after photos (if not already uploaded)            â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”œâ”€ Messages with client (screenshot)                        â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”œâ”€ GPS check-in/out data (auto-included)                    â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â””â”€ Additional notes/context                                 â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Suggests resolution (if any):                               â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”œâ”€ Accept partial refund (e.g., "I'll accept 20% refund")   â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”œâ”€ Offer to redo work (free cleaning)                       â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â””â”€ Deny dispute (explain why)                               â”‚
â”‚  â””â”€ Submits response                                            â”‚
â”‚                                                                 â”‚
â”‚  IF CLEANER DOESN'T RESPOND:                                    â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ After 24 hours: Reminder sent                               â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ After 48 hours: Auto-decided in client's favor              â”‚
â”‚  â””â”€ Cleaner loses opportunity to defend                         â”‚
â”‚                                                                 â”‚
â”‚  STEP 4: ADMIN REVIEW (2-5 Business Days)                       â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Assigned to admin investigator                              â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Reviews ALL evidence:                                       â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”œâ”€ Client's photos/description                              â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”œâ”€ Cleaner's photos/response                                â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”œâ”€ GPS check-in/out data:                                   â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”‚  â”œâ”€ Did cleaner arrive? (within 100m of address)          â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”‚  â”œâ”€ Was cleaner on time? (within 15min of start)          â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”‚  â”œâ”€ Did cleaner stay full time? (hours match booking)     â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”‚  â””â”€ GPS coordinates logged?                               â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”œâ”€ Message history:                                         â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”‚  â”œâ”€ Did cleaner communicate issues?                       â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”‚  â”œâ”€ Were there unreasonable client demands?               â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”‚  â””â”€ Tone/professionalism of both parties                  â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”œâ”€ Photo proof comparison:                                  â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”‚  â”œâ”€ Before photos: Show initial state                     â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”‚  â”œâ”€ After photos: Show completed work                     â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”‚  â””â”€ Side-by-side: Visible improvement?                    â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”œâ”€ Cleaner's reliability score:                             â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”‚  â”œâ”€ Current score (0-100)                                 â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”‚  â”œâ”€ Past disputes (any patterns?)                         â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”‚  â”œâ”€ Average rating (4.5+?)                                â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”‚  â””â”€ Total jobs (experienced?)                             â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”œâ”€ Client's booking history:                                â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”‚  â”œâ”€ Past disputes (serial complainer?)                    â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”‚  â”œâ”€ Average ratings given (too harsh?)                    â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”‚  â””â”€ Booking frequency (legitimate user?)                  â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â””â”€ Industry standards:                                      â”‚
â”‚  â”‚     â””â”€ What's reasonable to expect for this service type?    â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Makes decision based on evidence                            â”‚
â”‚  â””â”€ Documents reasoning (for transparency)                      â”‚
â”‚                                                                 â”‚
â”‚  STEP 5: DECISION COMMUNICATED (Email + SMS + Push)             â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Both parties notified simultaneously                        â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Decision options:                                           â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”œâ”€ FULL REFUND (100%)                                       â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”œâ”€ PARTIAL REFUND (25-75%)                                  â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”œâ”€ FREE REBOOK (0% refund, but new cleaner)                 â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â””â”€ DENY (0% refund, client charged)                         â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Reasoning explained (transparency)                          â”‚
â”‚  â””â”€ Next steps outlined                                         â”‚
â”‚                                                                 â”‚
â”‚  STEP 6: RESOLUTION EXECUTED                                    â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Credits refunded (if applicable)                            â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Cleaner paid remaining amount                               â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Reliability scores updated:                                 â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”œâ”€ Cleaner: -1 to -5 pts (if at fault)                      â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â””â”€ Client: Risk flag (if frivolous)                         â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Both can leave final comments                               â”‚
â”‚  â””â”€ Dispute closed                                              â”‚
â”‚                                                                 â”‚
â”‚  STEP 7: APPEALS (Optional, within 7 days)                      â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Either party can appeal decision                            â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Escalated to senior admin                                   â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Final decision (no further appeals)                         â”‚
â”‚  â””â”€ Rare (< 2% of disputes appealed)                            â”‚
â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜

### **Financial Responsibility Breakdown**

#### **WHO PAYS FOR WHAT?**

```
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚  ğŸ’° FINANCIAL RESPONSIBILITY MATRIX                             â”‚
â”œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¤
â”‚  SCENARIO 1: CLEANER'S FAULT (Legitimate Complaint)             â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Example: Cleaner did poor job, photos prove it              â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Decision: Partial refund (50%)                              â”‚
â”‚  â”‚                                                              â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  FINANCIAL FLOW:                                             â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”œâ”€ Booking total: 1,500 credits ($150)                      â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”œâ”€ Refund to client: 750 credits ($75)                      â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”œâ”€ Cleaner receives: 750 credits ($75)                      â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”‚  â”œâ”€ After 15% platform fee: $63.75                        â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”‚  â””â”€ Cleaner's final payout: $63.75                        â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â””â”€ Platform keeps: 15% of $75 = $11.25                      â”‚
â”‚  â”‚                                                              â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  WHO LOSES MONEY:                                            â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”œâ”€ Cleaner: Loses $75 (50% of earnings)                     â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”œâ”€ Platform: Loses $11.25 (50% of fee)                      â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â””â”€ Client: Gets $75 back (made whole)                       â”‚
â”‚  â”‚                                                              â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  WHY IT'S FAIR:                                              â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”œâ”€ Cleaner did poor work â†’ Cleaner pays                     â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”œâ”€ Platform enabled poor cleaner â†’ Platform shares cost     â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â””â”€ Client was wronged â†’ Client made whole                   â”‚
â”‚  â”‚                                                              â”‚
â”‚  â””â”€ RELIABILITY IMPACT:                                         â”‚
â”‚     â”œâ”€ Cleaner: -3 pts reliability score                        â”‚
â”‚     â”œâ”€ May drop to lower tier (loss of future earnings)         â”‚
â”‚     â””â”€ Pattern = deactivation                                   â”‚
â”‚                                                                 â”‚
â”œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¤

â”‚  â”‚                                                              â”‚

â”‚  â”‚  â”œâ”€ No one! Everyone gets what they're owed.                 â”‚

### **Explicit Refund Criteria**

#### **FULL REFUND (100%) - Criteria**

```
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚  ğŸ’¯ FULL REFUND SCENARIOS               â”‚
â”œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¤
â”‚  1. NO-SHOW (Cleaner Never Arrived)     â”‚
â”‚     â”œâ”€ GPS: No check-in recorded        â”‚
â”‚     â”œâ”€ Client: Waited at home           â”‚
â”‚     â”œâ”€ Photos: None submitted           â”‚
â”‚     â””â”€ Result: 100% refund + cleaner    â”‚
â”‚        banned                           â”‚
â”‚                                         â”‚
â”‚  2. SAFETY ISSUE (Theft, Assault)       â”‚
â”‚     â”œâ”€ Police report filed              â”‚
â”‚     â”œâ”€ Evidence of theft/damage         â”‚
â”‚     â”œâ”€ Immediate investigation          â”‚
â”‚     â””â”€ Result: 100% refund + $500       â”‚
â”‚        compensation + cleaner banned    â”‚
â”‚                                         â”‚
â”‚  3. NOT CLEANED AT ALL                  â”‚
â”‚     â”œâ”€ Before/after photos identical    â”‚
â”‚     â”œâ”€ GPS: Short check-in (< 30 min)   â”‚
â”‚     â”œâ”€ Clear evidence nothing done      â”‚
â”‚     â””â”€ Result: 100% refund + cleaner    â”‚
â”‚        deactivated                      â”‚
â”‚                                         â”‚
â”‚  4. PLATFORM ERROR (System Failure)     â”‚
â”‚     â”œâ”€ App crash prevented service      â”‚
â”‚     â”œâ”€ Payment processing error         â”‚
â”‚     â”œâ”€ Wrong cleaner sent               â”‚
â”‚     â””â”€ Result: 100% refund + $25        â”‚
â”‚        compensation                     â”‚
â”‚                                         â”‚
â”‚  5. SERIOUS QUALITY ISSUES              â”‚
â”‚     â”œâ”€ < 20% of agreed work completed   â”‚
â”‚     â”œâ”€ Photos prove major deficiencies  â”‚
â”‚     â”œâ”€ Multiple rooms not touched       â”‚
â”‚     â””â”€ Result: 100% refund + cleaner    â”‚
â”‚        suspended                        â”‚
â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜

#### **PARTIAL REFUND (25-75%) - Criteria**

```
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚  âš–ï¸ PARTIAL REFUND SCENARIOS            â”‚
â”œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¤
â”‚  1. MINOR QUALITY ISSUES (25% refund)   â”‚
â”‚     â”œâ”€ 1-2 small areas missed           â”‚
â”‚     â”œâ”€ Overall job is good              â”‚
â”‚     â”œâ”€ Photos show most work done       â”‚
â”‚     â””â”€ Example: "Forgot to clean 1      â”‚

## â­ CLEANER TIER BENEFITS - DETAILED EXPLANATION

### **Complete Tier Benefits Breakdown**

Each tier provides specific benefits that are automatically applied based on the cleaner's reliability score. Here's every benefit explained in detail:

#### **BENEFIT 1: BASE RATE RANGE**

**What It Means:**
The hourly rate range you're allowed to charge clients.

```
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚  ğŸ’° BASE RATE RANGES BY TIER                                    â”‚
â”œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¤
â”‚  ğŸŒ± DEVELOPING (Score 0-59):                                    â”‚

â”‚  â”œâ”€ How It Works:                                               â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”œâ”€ You can set your rate anywhere in this range             â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”œâ”€ Lower end attracts more bookings (price-sensitive)       â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”œâ”€ Higher end = fewer bookings but more per job             â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â””â”€ Most new cleaners start at $20-25/hr                     â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ How It's Enforced:                                          â”‚

â”‚  â”‚  â”œâ”€ Cannot enter $36/hr (outside range â†’ error)              â”‚

â”‚        build score, then increase rate                          â”‚

â”‚     â”œâ”€ 20 jobs/month Ã— 3 hours avg Ã— $40/hr = $2,400           â”‚

```

**How Rate Changes Are Applied:**
```javascript
// Backend enforcement
function validateCleanerRate(cleaner, proposedRate) {
  const tierRanges = {
    'Developing': { min: 150, max: 350 },
    'Semi Pro': { min: 350, max: 450 },
    'Pro': { min: 450, max: 600 },
    'Elite': { min: 600, max: 850 }
  };
  
  const range = tierRanges[cleaner.tier];
  
  if (proposedRate < range.min || proposedRate > range.max) {
    return {
      valid: false,
      error: `Your tier (${cleaner.tier}) allows rates between ${range.min}-${range.max} credits/hr. Proposed: ${proposedRate}.`
    };
  }
  
  return { valid: true };
}
```

### **How Tier Benefits Are Determined**

```
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚  ğŸ” TIER ASSIGNMENT PROCESS                                     â”‚
â”œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¤
â”‚  STEP 1: RELIABILITY SCORE CALCULATED                           â”‚
â”‚  â””â”€ After EVERY booking approval, score recalculated            â”‚
â”‚                                                                 â”‚
â”‚  STEP 2: SCORE MAPPED TO TIER                                   â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ 0-59: Developing                                            â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ 60-74: Semi Pro                                             â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ 75-89: Pro                                                  â”‚
â”‚  â””â”€ 90-100: Elite                                               â”‚
â”‚                                                                 â”‚
â”‚  STEP 3: TIER UPDATED IN DATABASE                               â”‚
â”‚  ```javascript                                                  â”‚
â”‚  function updateCleanerTier(cleaner) {                          â”‚
â”‚    const score = cleaner.reliability_score;                     â”‚
â”‚    let newTier;                                                 â”‚
â”‚    if (score >= 90) newTier = 'Elite';                          â”‚
â”‚    else if (score >= 75) newTier = 'Pro';                       â”‚
â”‚    else if (score >= 60) newTier = 'Semi Pro';                  â”‚
â”‚    else newTier = 'Developing';                                 â”‚
â”‚    cleaner.tier = newTier;                                      â”‚
â”‚    cleaner.save();                                              â”‚
â”‚  }                                                              â”‚
â”‚  ```                                                            â”‚
â”‚                                                                 â”‚
â”‚  STEP 4: BENEFITS AUTOMATICALLY APPLIED                         â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Rate range updated (dropdown options change)                â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Badge updated on profile                                    â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Match priority boost activated                              â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Support tier upgraded                                       â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Payout options unlocked                                     â”‚
â”‚  â””â”€ Featured listing (if Pro/Elite)                             â”‚
â”‚                                                                 â”‚
â”‚  STEP 5: CLEANER NOTIFIED                                       â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Email: "Congratulations! You're now Pro!"                   â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ SMS: "You've been promoted to Pro tier!"                    â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Push: "ğŸ‰ Tier upgrade! New benefits unlocked"              â”‚
â”‚  â””â”€ In-app banner: "Welcome to Pro tier!"                       â”‚
â”‚                                                                 â”‚
â”‚  TIMING: REAL-TIME (No delay!)                                  â”‚
â”‚  â””â”€ Benefits active within seconds of score update              â”‚
â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜

â”‚   can drop your tier, but good habits   â”‚
â”‚   bring it back quickly!"               â”‚
â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜
```

---

## ğŸ“Š DATA ARCHITECTURE (Complete Database Schema)

### **Overview**

PureTask uses Base44 (MongoDB-based BaaS) for all data storage. Here's the complete database schema with relationships, field types, indexes, and business logic.

### **Core Entities**

#### **1. Users (Base44 Auth Built-In)**

```javascript
// Base44 handles user authentication
User {
  _id: ObjectId,
  email: String (unique, indexed),
  user_type: Enum ['client', 'cleaner', 'admin'],
  role: Enum ['client', 'cleaner', 'admin'], // Base44 field
  created_at: DateTime,
  last_login: DateTime,
  email_verified: Boolean,
  phone_verified: Boolean,
  is_active: Boolean,
  deleted_at: DateTime (soft delete)
}
```

**Indexes:**
- `email` (unique)
- `user_type` (for filtering)
- `created_at` (for analytics)

---

#### **2. CleanerProfile**

```javascript
CleanerProfile {
  _id: ObjectId,
  user_email: String (FK â†’ User.email, indexed),
  
  // BASIC INFO
  full_name: String,
  phone: String,
  date_of_birth: Date,
  profile_photo_url: String (S3/Cloudinary),
  bio: String (max 500 chars),
  languages_spoken: Array<String>, // ['English', 'Spanish']
  years_experience: Number,
  
  // LOCATION & SERVICE AREA
  service_zip_codes: Array<String>, // ['90210', '90211', '90212']
  primary_address: String,
  latitude: Number,
  longitude: Number,
  max_travel_distance: Number (miles, default: 15),
  
  // PRICING (in credits)
  base_rate_credits_per_hour: Number, // 150-850 based on tier
  deep_addon_credits_per_hour: Number, // +40-80
  moveout_addon_credits_per_hour: Number, // +60-100
  additional_service_pricing: {
    oven: Number (credits),
    refrigerator: Number,
    windows: Number,
    laundry: Number,
    dishes: Number,
    cabinets: Number,
    garage: Number,
    balcony: Number
  },
  
  // TIER & PERFORMANCE
  tier: Enum ['Developing', 'Semi Pro', 'Pro', 'Elite'],
  reliability_score: Number (0-100, decimal),
  total_jobs: Number,
  jobs_completed: Number,
  jobs_cancelled: Number,
  jobs_no_show: Number,
  average_rating: Number (1.0-5.0),
  total_reviews: Number,
  
  // RELIABILITY COMPONENTS (Tracked for scoring)
  attendance_rate: Number (percentage, 0-100),
  on_time_rate: Number (percentage, 0-100),
  photo_compliance_rate: Number (percentage, 0-100),
  communication_rate: Number (percentage, 0-100),
  completion_confirmation_rate: Number (percentage, 0-100),
  cancellation_rate: Number (percentage, 0-100),
  no_show_rate: Number (percentage, 0-100),
  dispute_rate: Number (percentage, 0-100),
  
  // PREFERENCES
  specialty_tags: Array<String>, 
  // ['pets', 'eco_friendly', 'deep_clean', 'move_out', 
  //  'commercial', 'airbnb', 'post_construction', 'elderly_care']
  product_preference: Enum ['bring_own', 'use_clients', 'either'],
  brings_own_supplies: Boolean,
  pet_friendly: Boolean,
  eco_friendly_only: Boolean,
  
  // AVAILABILITY
  is_active: Boolean,
  is_accepting_jobs: Boolean,
  max_jobs_per_day: Number (default: 3),
  max_jobs_per_week: Number (default: 20),
  recurring_availability: {
    monday: Array<TimeSlot>, // [{start: '08:00', end: '17:00'}]
    tuesday: Array<TimeSlot>,
    wednesday: Array<TimeSlot>,
    thursday: Array<TimeSlot>,
    friday: Array<TimeSlot>,
    saturday: Array<TimeSlot>,
    sunday: Array<TimeSlot>
  },
  blackout_dates: Array<Date>, // Vacations
  accepts_same_day: Boolean,
  
  // PAYOUTS
  payout_percentage: Number (0.80-0.85, default: 0.85),
  stripe_account_id: String (Stripe Connect),
  bank_account_verified: Boolean,
  bank_account_last4: String,
  payout_schedule: Enum ['weekly', 'daily'], // Elite gets daily
  
  // VERIFICATION
  background_check_status: Enum ['pending', 'approved', 'rejected', 'expired'],
  background_check_date: DateTime,
  background_check_provider: String ('Checkr'),
  background_check_report_id: String,
  background_check_fee_paid: Boolean,
  background_check_fee_reimbursed: Boolean,
  identity_verified: Boolean,
  identity_verification_date: DateTime,
  verified_badge: Boolean, // Semi Pro+ get badge
  
  // ONBOARDING
  onboarding_completed: Boolean,
  onboarding_step: Number (1-5),
  onboarding_completed_at: DateTime,
  
  // ANALYTICS
  total_earnings_all_time: Number (USD),
  earnings_this_month: Number,
  earnings_last_month: Number,
  acceptance_rate: Number (percentage, 0-100),
  response_time_avg_minutes: Number,
  
  // METADATA
  created_at: DateTime,
  updated_at: DateTime,
  last_active: DateTime
}
```

**Indexes:**
- `user_email` (unique)
- `tier` (for filtering)
- `service_zip_codes` (for location search)
- `is_active` + `is_accepting_jobs` (compound, for matching)
- `reliability_score` (for sorting)
- `average_rating` (for sorting)
- `specialty_tags` (multikey, for filtering)

---

#### **3. ClientProfile**

```javascript
ClientProfile {
  _id: ObjectId,
  user_email: String (FK â†’ User.email, indexed),
  
  // BASIC INFO
  full_name: String,
  phone: String,
  profile_photo_url: String,
  
  // PRIMARY ADDRESS
  default_address: String,
  apartment_unit: String,
  city: String,
  state: String,
  zip_code: String,
  latitude: Number,
  longitude: Number,
  
  // ADDITIONAL ADDRESSES (Multiple properties)
  additional_addresses: Array<{
    address: String,
    apartment_unit: String,
    city: String,
    state: String,
    zip_code: String,
    latitude: Number,
    longitude: Number,
    nickname: String, // 'Beach House', 'Airbnb #1'
    is_default: Boolean
  }>,
  
  // HOME DETAILS (Default property)
  bedrooms: Number,
  bathrooms: Number,
  square_feet: Number,
  home_type: Enum ['apartment', 'house', 'condo', 'townhouse', 'office'],
  has_pets: Boolean, // â­ TRIGGERS $30 FEE
  pet_types: Array<String>, // ['dog', 'cat', 'bird']
  parking_available: Boolean,
  parking_type: Enum ['driveway', 'street', 'garage', 'parking_lot'],
  entry_method: Enum ['meet_at_door', 'key_under_mat', 'lockbox', 'doorman'],
  
  // PREFERENCES
  preferred_specialty_tags: Array<String>,
  preferred_product_type: Enum ['eco_friendly', 'standard', 'bring_own', 'any'],
  product_allergies: String, // 'Bleach, ammonia'
  special_instructions: String, // 'Dog is friendly', 'Use side entrance'
  preferred_cleaner_gender: Enum ['any', 'female', 'male'],
  preferred_communication: Enum ['sms', 'email', 'phone', 'app'],
  
  // CREDITS & PAYMENTS
  credit_balance: Number (credits, not USD),
  total_credits_purchased: Number,
  total_credits_spent: Number,
  total_credits_earned: Number (referrals + loyalty),
  stripe_customer_id: String,
  default_payment_method_id: String (Stripe),
  auto_refill_enabled: Boolean,
  auto_refill_threshold: Number (default: 100 credits),
  auto_refill_amount: Number (default: 500 credits),
  
  // BOOKING HISTORY
  total_bookings: Number,
  bookings_completed: Number,
  bookings_cancelled: Number,
  last_booking_date: DateTime,
  last_booked_cleaner: String (cleaner_email),
  average_booking_value: Number (credits),
  
  // MEMBERSHIP
  membership_tier: Enum ['basic', 'premium', 'vip'],
  membership_status: Enum ['active', 'cancelled', 'expired'],
  membership_start_date: DateTime,
  membership_expiry_date: DateTime,
  stripe_subscription_id: String,
  auto_renew: Boolean,
  
  // LOYALTY
  loyalty_points: Number,
  loyalty_points_earned_all_time: Number,
  loyalty_points_redeemed_all_time: Number,
  loyalty_tier: Number (1-5, based on total bookings),
  
  // REFERRALS
  referral_code: String (unique, e.g., 'SARAH2026'),
  referred_by: String (referrer's email),
  total_referrals_sent: Number,
  total_referrals_completed: Number, // Completed first booking
  
  // FAVORITES & BLOCKS
  favorite_cleaners: Array<String>, // Array of cleaner emails
  blocked_cleaners: Array<String>,
  
  // RISK & QUALITY
  risk_score: Number (0-100, fraud detection),
  total_disputes_filed: Number,
  disputes_won: Number,
  disputes_lost: Number,
  average_rating_given: Number (1.0-5.0),
  is_high_value_client: Boolean, // VIP treatment flag
  
  // ONBOARDING
  onboarding_completed: Boolean,
  onboarding_step: Number (1-3),
  welcome_credit_granted: Boolean,
  
  // METADATA
  created_at: DateTime,
  updated_at: DateTime,
  last_active: DateTime
}
```

**Indexes:**
- `user_email` (unique)
- `zip_code` (for location matching)
- `membership_tier` (for features)
- `referral_code` (unique)
- `credit_balance` (for low balance notifications)

---

#### **4. Booking (CORE ENTITY)**

```javascript
Booking {
  _id: ObjectId,
  booking_number: String (unique, e.g., 'BK-2026-00123'),
  
  // PARTIES
  client_email: String (FK â†’ ClientProfile, indexed),
  cleaner_email: String (FK â†’ CleanerProfile, indexed),
  
  // BOOKING DETAILS
  cleaning_type: Enum ['basic', 'deep', 'moveout'],
  service_date: Date,
  start_time: String ('10:00'),
  end_time: String ('13:00'),
  hours: Number (decimal, e.g., 3.5),
  
  // LOCATION
  address: String,
  apartment_unit: String,
  city: String,
  state: String,
  zip_code: String,
  latitude: Number,
  longitude: Number,
  
  // HOME DETAILS
  bedrooms: Number,
  bathrooms: Number,
  square_feet: Number,
  home_type: String,
  has_pets: Boolean, // â­ TRIGGERS $30 FEE
  pet_types: Array<String>,
  
  // INSTRUCTIONS
  parking_instructions: String,
  entry_instructions: String,
  special_requests: String,
  product_preferences: String,
  product_allergies: String,
  
  // ADDITIONAL SERVICES
  additional_services: {
    oven: Number (quantity),
    refrigerator: Number,
    windows: Number,
    laundry: Boolean,
    dishes: Boolean,
    cabinets: Boolean,
    garage: Boolean,
    balcony: Boolean
  },
  
  // PRICING BREAKDOWN
  base_rate_credits: Number, // Cleaner's rate Ã— hours
  addon_rate_credits: Number, // Deep/moveout addon Ã— hours
  hourly_credits_total: Number, // base + addon
  additional_services_credits: Number,
  pet_fee_credits: Number, // â­ 300 credits ($30) if has_pets
  subtotal_credits: Number,
  discount_credits: Number, // Membership, promo, bundle
  discount_reason: String,
  bundle_discount_percent: Number,
  final_price_credits: Number,
  
  // PAYMENT
  payment_status: Enum [
    'pending', // Draft, not submitted
    'hold', // Credits held, awaiting cleaner acceptance
    'authorized', // Cleaner accepted, credits still held
    'charged', // Client approved, credits charged
    'refunded', // Full/partial refund
    'failed' // Payment failed
  ],
  stripe_payment_intent_id: String,
  payment_hold_at: DateTime,
  payment_charged_at: DateTime,
  refund_amount_credits: Number,
  refund_reason: String,
  
  // STATUS TRACKING
  status: Enum [
    'draft', // Client creating
    'awaiting_cleaner', // Submitted, waiting for acceptance
    'accepted', // Cleaner accepted
    'declined', // Cleaner declined
    'cancelled', // Either party cancelled
    'scheduled', // Confirmed, upcoming
    'on_the_way', // Cleaner en route
    'in_progress', // Cleaner checked in
    'completed', // Cleaner checked out
    'awaiting_approval', // Client reviewing (18hr window) â­
    'approved', // Client approved
    'disputed', // Client opened dispute
    'resolved', // Dispute resolved
    'expired' // No response within 24 hours
  ],
  
  // TIMESTAMPS (Lifecycle)
  created_at: DateTime,
  submitted_at: DateTime,
  cleaner_response_deadline: DateTime, // 24hrs from submission
  accepted_at: DateTime,
  declined_at: DateTime,
  cancelled_at: DateTime,
  cancellation_reason: String,
  cancelled_by: Enum ['client', 'cleaner', 'admin'],
  
  // GPS TRACKING
  check_in_time: DateTime,
  check_in_latitude: Number,
  check_in_longitude: Number,
  check_in_distance_from_address: Number (meters),
  check_out_time: DateTime,
  check_out_latitude: Number,
  check_out_longitude: Number,
  actual_hours_worked: Number, // Check-out minus check-in
  
  // PHOTO VERIFICATION
  before_photo_urls: Array<String>, // S3 URLs
  after_photo_urls: Array<String>,
  photos_submitted_at: DateTime,
  photos_approved: Boolean,
  
  // CLIENT APPROVAL (18-hour window â­)
  awaiting_approval_since: DateTime,
  auto_approval_deadline: DateTime, // +18 hours â­
  approved_at: DateTime,
  approved_by: Enum ['client', 'auto'], // Auto after 18hrs
  approval_notes: String,
  
  // CLEANER PAYOUT
  cleaner_earnings_credits: Number, // final_price Ã— 0.85
  cleaner_earnings_usd: Number,
  platform_fee_credits: Number, // final_price Ã— 0.15
  platform_fee_usd: Number,
  payout_status: Enum ['pending', 'batched', 'paid'],
  payout_id: String (FK â†’ Payout),
  payout_date: DateTime,
  
  // RECURRING
  is_recurring: Boolean,
  recurring_booking_id: String (FK â†’ RecurringBooking),
  
  // MULTI-BOOKING
  is_multi_booking: Boolean,
  booking_group_id: String (FK â†’ BookingGroup),
  
  // FLAGS
  is_first_booking: Boolean, // Client's first booking
  is_favorite_cleaner: Boolean,
  same_day_booking: Boolean,
  vip_client: Boolean,
  
  // METADATA
  updated_at: DateTime,
  completed_at: DateTime
}
```

**Indexes:**
- `booking_number` (unique)
- `client_email` + `service_date` (compound, for client dashboard)
- `cleaner_email` + `service_date` (compound, for cleaner calendar)
- `status` (for filtering)
- `service_date` + `status` (compound, for upcoming jobs)
- `auto_approval_deadline` (for cron job)

---

#### **5. Review**

```javascript
Review {
  _id: ObjectId,
  booking_id: String (FK â†’ Booking, indexed, unique),
  
  // PARTIES
  client_email: String,
  cleaner_email: String,
  
  // RATING
  rating: Number (1-5, required),
  
  // REVIEW CONTENT
  comment: String (max 1000 chars),
  tags: Array<String>, 
  // ['punctual', 'thorough', 'friendly', 'professional', 
  //  'efficient', 'detail_oriented', 'respectful']
  
  // PHOTOS (Optional, client can upload)
  photo_urls: Array<String>,
  
  // BOOLEAN QUESTIONS
  would_rebook: Boolean,
  met_expectations: Boolean,
  
  // PRIVATE FEEDBACK (Admin only)
  private_feedback: String,
  flagged_for_review: Boolean,
  flag_reason: String,
  
  // RESPONSE (Cleaner can respond)
  cleaner_response: String,
  cleaner_response_at: DateTime,
  
  // MODERATION
  is_published: Boolean,
  is_featured: Boolean, // Admin can feature excellent reviews
  helpful_count: Number, // Other users can mark as helpful
  
  // METADATA
  created_at: DateTime,
  updated_at: DateTime
}
```

**Indexes:**
- `booking_id` (unique)
- `cleaner_email` + `created_at` (compound, for profile reviews)
- `rating` (for filtering high-rated cleaners)
- `is_published` (for public display)

---

#### **6. CreditTransaction**

```javascript
CreditTransaction {
  _id: ObjectId,
  transaction_id: String (unique, e.g., 'TXN-2026-00123'),
  
  // USER
  user_email: String (indexed),
  user_type: Enum ['client', 'cleaner'],
  
  // TRANSACTION DETAILS
  amount: Number (credits, positive = credit, negative = debit),
  type: Enum [
    'purchase', // Client bought credits
    'booking_charge', // Client paid for booking
    'booking_refund', // Refund to client
    'promotional', // Platform granted promo credits
    'referral_reward', // Referral bonus
    'loyalty_redemption', // Loyalty points â†’ credits
    'compensation', // Service recovery
    'admin_adjustment', // Manual admin change
    'membership_bonus' // Monthly membership bonus
  ],
  
  // DESCRIPTION
  description: String,
  
  // RELATED ENTITIES
  booking_id: String (FK â†’ Booking, if applicable),
  stripe_charge_id: String (if purchase),
  stripe_refund_id: String (if refund),
  referral_code: String (if referral),
  admin_user_email: String (if admin action),
  
  // BALANCE TRACKING
  balance_before: Number (credits),
  balance_after: Number (credits),
  
  // EXPIRATION (Promotional credits only)
  expires_at: DateTime,
  
  // METADATA
  created_at: DateTime,
  notes: String
}
```

**Indexes:**
- `transaction_id` (unique)
- `user_email` + `created_at` (compound, for transaction history)
- `type` (for analytics)
- `expires_at` (for expiration cron job)

---

#### **7. Payout**

```javascript
Payout {
  _id: ObjectId,
  payout_id: String (unique, e.g., 'PO-2026-00123'),
  
  // CLEANER
  cleaner_email: String (indexed),
  
  // PAYOUT DETAILS
  amount_usd: Number (decimal, e.g., 612.80),
  booking_ids: Array<String>, // All bookings in this payout
  booking_count: Number,
  
  // STATUS
  status: Enum [
    'pending', // Awaiting approval, within 18hr window
    'approved', // Ready for batch
    'batched', // Included in weekly/daily batch
    'processing', // Sent to Stripe
    'paid', // Completed
    'failed', // Stripe transfer failed
    'cancelled' // Admin cancelled
  ],
  
  // STRIPE
  stripe_transfer_id: String,
  stripe_account_id: String,
  
  // INSTANT CASH-OUT â­
  is_instant_cashout: Boolean,
  instant_cashout_fee_percent: Number (10), // â­ 10% fee
  instant_cashout_fee_amount: Number,
  net_amount_after_fee: Number,
  
  // BATCH INFO
  batch_id: String, // Weekly batch identifier
  batch_date: Date, // Friday for weekly, daily for Elite
  
  // TIMESTAMPS
  created_at: DateTime,
  approved_at: DateTime,
  processed_at: DateTime,
  paid_at: DateTime,
  
  // FAILURE HANDLING
  failure_reason: String,
  retry_count: Number,
  next_retry_at: DateTime
}
```

**Indexes:**
- `payout_id` (unique)
- `cleaner_email` + `status` (compound)
- `batch_id` (for batch processing)
- `status` + `created_at` (compound, for pending payouts)

---

#### **8. Dispute**

```javascript
Dispute {
  _id: ObjectId,
  dispute_id: String (unique, e.g., 'DSP-2026-00123'),
  
  // RELATED ENTITIES
  booking_id: String (FK â†’ Booking, indexed, unique),
  client_email: String,
  cleaner_email: String,
  
  // DISPUTE DETAILS
  reason: Enum [
    'no_show',
    'quality_issue',
    'late_arrival',
    'incomplete_work',
    'damage',
    'wrong_products_used',
    'cleaner_unprofessional',
    'other'
  ],
  description: String (max 1000 chars),
  evidence_photo_urls: Array<String>,
  evidence_video_urls: Array<String>,
  
  // REQUESTED RESOLUTION
  requested_resolution: Enum [
    'full_refund',
    'partial_refund',
    'free_rebook',
    'other'
  ],
  requested_refund_amount: Number (credits),
  
  // CLEANER RESPONSE
  cleaner_response: String,
  cleaner_response_at: DateTime,
  cleaner_evidence_urls: Array<String>,
  cleaner_response_deadline: DateTime, // 24hrs from filing
  
  // ADMIN REVIEW
  assigned_to_admin: String (admin email),
  admin_reviewed_at: DateTime,
  admin_notes: String,
  
  // DECISION
  status: Enum [
    'open', // Just filed
    'awaiting_cleaner', // Waiting for cleaner response
    'under_review', // Admin investigating
    'resolved', // Decision made
    'closed', // Final (after any appeals)
    'appealed' // Party appealed decision
  ],
  resolution: Enum [
    'full_refund', // 100%
    'partial_refund', // 25-75%
    'free_rebook', // New booking
    'deny' // No refund
  ],
  refund_percent: Number (0-100),
  refund_amount_credits: Number,
  resolution_reasoning: String, // Why this decision
  
  // APPEAL
  appeal_filed_by: Enum ['client', 'cleaner'],
  appeal_reason: String,
  appeal_filed_at: DateTime,
  appeal_reviewed_by: String (senior admin),
  appeal_decision: String,
  appeal_final: Boolean,
  
  // IMPACT ON RELIABILITY SCORE
  cleaner_score_penalty: Number (-5 to 0),
  client_risk_flag_added: Boolean,
  
  // TIMESTAMPS
  created_at: DateTime,
  resolved_at: DateTime,
  closed_at: DateTime,
  
  // ESCALATION
  escalated: Boolean,
  escalation_reason: String,
  priority: Enum ['low', 'normal', 'high', 'urgent']
}
```

**Indexes:**
- `dispute_id` (unique)
- `booking_id` (unique)
- `status` (for filtering)
- `assigned_to_admin` (for admin dashboard)
- `created_at` (for sorting)

---

#### **9. RecurringBooking**

```javascript
RecurringBooking {
  _id: ObjectId,
  recurring_id: String (unique, e.g., 'REC-2026-00123'),
  
  // PARTIES
  client_email: String (indexed),
  cleaner_email: String (indexed),
  
  // SCHEDULE
  frequency: Enum ['weekly', 'biweekly', 'monthly'],
  day_of_week: Enum ['monday', 'tuesday', ..., 'sunday'],
  start_time: String ('10:00'),
  hours: Number,
  
  // BOOKING TEMPLATE
  cleaning_type: Enum ['basic', 'deep', 'moveout'],
  address: String,
  latitude: Number,
  longitude: Number,
  home_details: Object, // Same as Booking schema
  special_requests: String,
  additional_services: Object,
  
  // PRICING (Locked in at setup)
  base_rate_credits: Number,
  addon_rate_credits: Number,
  hourly_credits_total: Number,
  additional_services_credits: Number,
  pet_fee_credits: Number, // â­ 300 if has_pets
  recurring_discount_percent: Number (10), // 10% discount
  final_price_per_booking: Number (credits),
  
  // SCHEDULE DATES
  start_date: Date, // First occurrence
  end_date: Date (nullable), // If set end date
  next_occurrence: Date, // Next auto-generated booking
  
  // STATUS
  status: Enum [
    'active', // Auto-generating bookings
    'paused', // Temporarily stopped
    'cancelled', // Ended by client/cleaner
    'completed' // Reached end date
  ],
  paused_until: Date,
  pause_reason: String,
  cancellation_reason: String,
  
  // GENERATED BOOKINGS
  total_bookings_generated: Number,
  total_bookings_completed: Number,
  generated_booking_ids: Array<String>, // All auto-created bookings
  
  // AUTO-GENERATION SETTINGS
  auto_generate_days_advance: Number (7), // Create 7 days before
  auto_accept_by_cleaner: Boolean, // Skip acceptance step
  
  // MODIFICATION
  allow_modifications: Boolean,
  modification_notice_hours: Number (24), // How far in advance
  
  // SKIP DATES
  skipped_dates: Array<Date>, // Client manually skipped
  skip_reasons: Object, // {date: reason}
  
  // METADATA
  created_at: DateTime,
  updated_at: DateTime,
  last_booking_generated_at: DateTime,
  cancelled_at: DateTime
}
```

**Indexes:**
- `recurring_id` (unique)
- `client_email` + `status` (compound)
- `next_occurrence` (for cron job generation)
- `status` (for filtering active)

---

#### **10. Notification**

```javascript
Notification {
  _id: ObjectId,
  
  // RECIPIENT
  user_email: String (indexed),
  user_type: Enum ['client', 'cleaner', 'admin'],
  
  // NOTIFICATION DETAILS
  type: Enum [
    'booking_accepted',
    'booking_declined',
    'booking_cancelled',
    'booking_reminder', // 24hrs before
    'cleaner_on_way',
    'cleaner_checked_in',
    'cleaner_checked_out',
    'approval_needed', // Review photos
    'auto_approval_soon', // 3hrs before 18hr deadline â­
    'auto_approved', // After 18hrs â­
    'payment_charged',
    'payout_processed',
    'review_left',
    'dispute_opened',
    'dispute_resolved',
    'message_received',
    'credit_low', // Balance < 100
    'membership_expiring',
    'referral_completed',
    'tier_promoted',
    'tier_demoted',
    'system_announcement'
  ],
  
  // CONTENT
  title: String,
  message: String,
  action_url: String, // Deep link
  action_text: String, // Button text
  
  // CHANNELS
  send_email: Boolean,
  send_sms: Boolean,
  send_push: Boolean,
  send_in_app: Boolean,
  
  // DELIVERY STATUS
  email_sent: Boolean,
  email_opened: Boolean,
  email_clicked: Boolean,
  sms_sent: Boolean,
  push_sent: Boolean,
  push_clicked: Boolean,
  in_app_read: Boolean,
  
  // PRIORITY
  priority: Enum ['low', 'normal', 'high', 'urgent'],
  
  // RELATED ENTITY
  booking_id: String (FK â†’ Booking, if applicable),
  dispute_id: String,
  payout_id: String,
  
  // METADATA
  created_at: DateTime,
  sent_at: DateTime,
  read_at: DateTime,
  expires_at: DateTime, // Auto-delete old notifications
  
  // BATCHING (Prevent spam)
  batch_key: String, // Group related notifications
  is_batched: Boolean
}
```

**Indexes:**
- `user_email` + `created_at` (compound, for user notifications)
- `type` (for analytics)
- `in_app_read` + `created_at` (compound, for unread count)
- `expires_at` (for cleanup cron job)

### **Relationships Diagram**

```
User (email)
  â”œâ”€â”€â”€ ClientProfile (user_email)
  â”‚      â”œâ”€â”€â”€ Booking (client_email)
  â”‚      â”œâ”€â”€â”€ Review (client_email)
  â”‚      â”œâ”€â”€â”€ CreditTransaction (user_email)
  â”‚      â”œâ”€â”€â”€ Notification (user_email)
  â”‚      â””â”€â”€â”€ RecurringBooking (client_email)
  â”‚
  â””â”€â”€â”€ CleanerProfile (user_email)
         â”œâ”€â”€â”€ Booking (cleaner_email)
         â”œâ”€â”€â”€ Review (cleaner_email)
         â”œâ”€â”€â”€ Payout (cleaner_email)
         â”œâ”€â”€â”€ Notification (user_email)
         â””â”€â”€â”€ RecurringBooking (cleaner_email)

Booking
  â”œâ”€â”€â”€ Review (booking_id, unique)
  â”œâ”€â”€â”€ Dispute (booking_id, unique)
  â”œâ”€â”€â”€ CreditTransaction (booking_id)
  â””â”€â”€â”€ RecurringBooking (generates multiple Bookings)

Dispute
  â””â”€â”€â”€ Booking (dispute.booking_id â†’ booking._id)

Payout
  â””â”€â”€â”€ Bookings (payout.booking_ids[] â†’ booking._id[])
```

## ğŸ“ˆ BUSINESS METRICS & KPIs

### **North Star Metrics**

#### **1. Gross Merchandise Value (GMV)**
```
Definition: Total $ value of all bookings
Formula: Sum of all booking final prices (USD)
Target: $5M Year 1 â†’ $20M Year 2 â†’ $50M Year 3

Monthly Breakdown (Year 1):
â”œâ”€ Month 1-3: $150K/month avg ($450K total)
â”œâ”€ Month 4-6: $350K/month avg ($1.05M total)
â”œâ”€ Month 7-9: $550K/month avg ($1.65M total)
â”œâ”€ Month 10-12: $800K/month avg ($2.4M total)
â””â”€ TOTAL YEAR 1: $5.55M GMV

Why It Matters:
â”œâ”€ Measures platform usage
â”œâ”€ Indicates market fit
â””â”€ Drives all other revenue metrics
```

#### **2. Take Rate (Platform Revenue %)**
```
Definition: Platform fee as % of GMV
Formula: (Platform Fees / GMV) Ã— 100
Current: 15% baseline
Target: Maintain 15-20%

Revenue Calculation:
â”œâ”€ Year 1 GMV: $5.55M Ã— 15% = $832,500 platform fees
â”œâ”€ Additional revenue:
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Pet fees (40% of bookings): $720K
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Instant cash-outs (10% fee): $360K â­
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Memberships: $180K
â”‚  â””â”€ Bundle offers: $80K
â””â”€ TOTAL YEAR 1: $2.17M revenue

Why It Matters:
â”œâ”€ Direct revenue metric
â”œâ”€ Benchmark: Uber (25%), TaskRabbit (15%)
â””â”€ Higher = Better unit economics
```

#### **3. Net Revenue Retention (NRR)**
```
Definition: Revenue retention + expansion from cohort
Formula: (Starting MRR + Expansion - Churn) / Starting MRR Ã— 100
Target: 120%+ (with upsells/cross-sells)

Example (Month 12 Cohort):
â”œâ”€ Jan cohort: 100 clients, $50K MRR
â”œâ”€ Dec same cohort:
â”‚  â”œâ”€ 85 still active (15% churn)
â”‚  â”œâ”€ 30 upgraded to Premium/VIP
â”‚  â”œâ”€ 40 increased booking frequency
â”‚  â””â”€ Revenue: $65K MRR (30% growth!)
â””â”€ NRR: $65K / $50K = 130% âœ…

Why It Matters:
â”œâ”€ Measures growth without new users
â”œâ”€ 100%+ = Negative churn (ideal)
â””â”€ Key metric for SaaS/marketplace valuations
```

#### **Client Lifetime Value (LTV)**
```
Definition: Total revenue from client over lifetime
Formula: Avg booking value Ã— Bookings per month Ã— Avg lifetime months
Target: $500-800

Calculation Example:
â”œâ”€ Average booking: $150
â”œâ”€ Bookings per month: 1.8
â”œâ”€ Average lifetime: 24 months
â”œâ”€ LTV: $150 Ã— 1.8 Ã— 24 = $6,480
â”œâ”€ Platform revenue (15%): $972
â””â”€ Actual LTV: $972 âœ…

LTV by Segment:
â”œâ”€ Basic (Free): $420
â”œâ”€ Premium ($9.99/mo): $680
â”œâ”€ VIP ($19.99/mo): $1,240
â””â”€ Airbnb Power Users: $3,500+

Why It Matters:
â”œâ”€ LTV > CAC = Profitable
â”œâ”€ LTV:CAC ratio: 
â”‚  â”œâ”€ 1:1 = Break-even (bad)
â”‚  â”œâ”€ 3:1 = Good
â”‚  â”œâ”€ 5:1 = Excellent
â”‚  â””â”€ 10:1 = Exceptional (referrals)
â””â”€ Informs max CAC spend
```

#### **LTV:CAC Ratio**
```
Definition: Lifetime value divided by acquisition cost
Formula: LTV / CAC
Target: 10:1 (marketplace standard)
Current: Track monthly

Example:
â”œâ”€ LTV: $972 (from above)
â”œâ”€ CAC: $40 (from above)
â””â”€ Ratio: $972 / $40 = 24:1 ğŸ‰ (Exceptional!)

Why 24:1 Is Possible:
â”œâ”€ High repeat rate (60%+)
â”œâ”€ Low churn (loyal clients)
â”œâ”€ Referral program (low CAC)
â”œâ”€ Membership upsells (increases LTV)
â””â”€ Network effects (organic growth)

Benchmark:
â”œâ”€ 1:1 = Unsustainable
â”œâ”€ 3:1 = Minimum viable
â”œâ”€ 5:1 = Healthy business
â”œâ”€ 10:1 = Venture-scale
â””â”€ 20:1+ = Unicorn potential ğŸ¦„
```

#### **Revenue Metrics**

â”œâ”€ Compounding growth
â””â”€ Reduces customer acquisition pressure

##### **Booking Revenue vs Other Revenue**

##### **Revenue Per Booking**
```
Definition: Platform revenue per completed booking
Formula: Total platform fees / Completed bookings

â”œâ”€ Average booking: $150 total
â”œâ”€ Platform fee (15%): $22.50
â”œâ”€ Pet fee (40% of bookings): $30 Ã— 0.4 = $12
â”œâ”€ Total per booking: $22.50 + $12 = $34.50 âœ…

â”œâ”€ Upsell add-ons (oven, windows) = +$5/booking
â”œâ”€ Membership discounts = -$2/booking (worth it for retention)
â””â”€ Net effect: $37.50/booking target by Year 2
```

##### **Gross Margin**
```
Definition: (Revenue - COGS) / Revenue Ã— 100
Target: 75%+

COGS (Cost of Goods Sold):
â”œâ”€ Stripe fees (2.9% + $0.30)
â”œâ”€ Twilio SMS ($0.0079/message)
â”œâ”€ SendGrid email ($0.00095/email)
â”œâ”€ Google Maps API ($5/1000 requests)
â”œâ”€ Background checks ($35, but reimbursed)
â””â”€ Total: ~5% of revenue

Calculation:
â”œâ”€ Revenue: $2.17M
â”œâ”€ COGS: $108K (5%)
â”œâ”€ Gross Profit: $2.06M
â””â”€ Gross Margin: 95%! ğŸ‰

Why So High?
â”œâ”€ Marketplace model (low COGS)
â”œâ”€ No inventory
â”œâ”€ No physical fulfillment
â””â”€ Software scales infinitely
```

#### **Cost Metrics**

##### **CAC Payback Period**
```

Formula: CAC / (Monthly revenue per client)
Target: <6 months

Calculation:
â”œâ”€ CAC: $40
â”œâ”€ Monthly revenue per client:

â”‚  â”œâ”€ $34.50 platform revenue/booking
â”‚  â””â”€ $62/month
â”œâ”€ Payback: $40 / $62 = 0.65 months âœ…
â””â”€ Result: Payback in 20 days! (Excellent!)

Benchmark:
â”œâ”€ <3 months: Excellent
â”œâ”€ 3-6 months: Good
â”œâ”€ 6-12 months: Acceptable
â””â”€ >12 months: Concerning (burning cash)
```

## ğŸš€ STRATEGIC RECOMMENDATIONS (Detailed)

### **A. Immediate Optimizations (0-3 Months)**

#### **1. Conversion Funnel Optimization**

**Current Funnel (Assumed):**
```

â†“ 40% proceed

â†“ 50% select

â†“ 60% complete

â†“ 90% approve

```
